The good place is that the rooms are arranged exactly according to my requirements, quiet, smoke-free, and close to the elevator. The bed in the standard room is large enough, 1.5 meters, to sleep with me and my baby without stress.
The downside is that
First, it should be checked in at 2 pm, but when I came to the hotel it was more than 4 pm and was told that the room had not been cleaned.
Second, when I came back at 11:30 in the evening, the welcome fruit had not been delivered yet, and it was delivered after I called.
Third, the room facilities are average, the TV is small, there are no childrenâ€™s slippers, and the toiletries are inferior. It is recommended that you donâ€™t use them. I think the online evaluation is Borghese, so there is no toiletries, so the experience is very bad.
Fourth, the service did not surprise me. Because it was late to watch the performance at the Shaanxi Grand Theater in the evening, I couldnâ€™t call the car and it started to rain. I took my two children and called the hotel in desperation, hoping to get a car for me, but the hotel I only express regret. I can only call a car to the airport. It costs 150 yuan for a 10-minute journey. After I hung up the phone, I wanted to call a car from the hotel, but I couldn't get it right at the time and finally walked back. It may be better if the hotel has a sense of ownership and flexible handling. However, the service consciousness of northerners may not be very strong, and they understand it. After all, the people who answer the phone are only working people, and there is no need to do extra things.
